2026-06-28T17:02:36Z [PLANNER_RESPONSE]: Ah, I know exactly what happened here!

You are seeing broken images because when you uploaded the image, the application was generating a temporary **Blob URL** (like `blob:http://localhost:3000/...`) and saving *that temporary string* directly to the database. Blob URLs are strictly temporary and only exist in the memory of the browser tab that created them. The moment you refresh the page or restart the app, the browser clears that memory, making the database string point to a dead link!
